msg:I came to the Millennium Yandu-Yancheng for the first time because of a business trip. I hesitated between Hilton and Marriott before moving in. Finally, considering the distance from the factory I was going to, I finally chose Hilton. .
Geographical location:
The hotel is located in the Financial Street of Yandu District, which belongs to the new district. The road is spacious, the vision is wide, and the quietness in the midst of the hustle and bustle. Next to it is Chuanchang River, not far from Yandu Park and Julong Lake Park. It is convenient for running and exercising in the morning. They are all plastic tracks and have a first-class environment. It is also very close to the Haiyan Museum, and it is also convenient to eat around. There are many restaurants with North Jiangsu specialties and Huaiyang cuisine.
hotel service
With five-star service ğŸ‘ğŸ» I have stayed at Hilton Hotel before on business trips, but the service is uneven. But Hilton Yancheng's service is very good, and the details are in place. As soon as the car arrived at the door of the hotel, someone came to open the door and take luggage. When checking in, because there were many people at that time, the manager of the hotel deer took the initiative to come over to check in and carefully instructed every matter and sent it all the way to the elevator. When I checked out, Ms. Yang at the front desk learned that I was going to Yancheng Station and took the initiative to call for a taxi. On the day of check-out, when Ms.Lynn from the front desk of the hotel came to visit by phone, I learned that I had never received the membership registration email, and immediately resolved the matter. The efficiency is very highğŸ‘ğŸ», and I can really feel the enthusiasm and responsibility for customers.
Hotel facilities
The hotel opened in 2021, with brand-new facilities and a high degree of intelligence. For so many years, I have always believed that the beds and pillows of Hilton Hotel are the most comfortable, and the three-day stay is the best sleep during this period. Also the room was cleaned quickly. Then there is the Chinese restaurant on the 4th floor, which is mainly Huaiyang cuisine and also integrates other cuisines, and the customers are also very satisfied. In short, the next time you come to Yancheng Hilton should be the only choice.
